[30;1m196 | [0m[35m#### CardanoShelley library[0m
[30;1m197 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m198 | [0m[35mThe `CardanoShelley` class allows getting addresses and staking addresses from a `Cip1852` object.\[0m
[30;1m199 | [0m[35mSince the staking address depends on the account index, the `Cip1852` object used to construct it sh[0m
[30;1m200 | [0m[35m(i.e. the account keys shall already be derived).\[0m
[30;1m201 | [0m[35mOnce constructed, it allows deriving change and address indexes like the `Cip1852` class, but it int[0m
[30;1m202 | [0m[35mof the staking keys.\[0m
